CHOS KYI PHYED DANG GANG DAG NI, ,BCU GNYIS NANG GIR BSHAD DBANG\
PO, ,ZHES BYUNG, ,SHES BYA CHOS CAN, BCO BRGYAD LAS DBANG PO YIN\
MIN GYI KHYAD PAR YOD DE, CHOS\
\
@106B KHAMS KYI PHYED MDO LAS BSHAD PA'I SROG GI DBANG PO DANG\
TSOR BDE SOGS LNGA DANG DAD SOGS LNGA DANG, BCU GNYIS MI SHES PO\
GSUM KYI CHA RE STE BCU BZHI DANG, NANG GI KHAMS BCU GNYIS PA'I\
DBANG\
\
PO GSUM KYI CHA RE STE BCU BZHI DANG, NANG GI KHAMS BCU GNYIS TE,\
DE DAG DBANG PO YIN LA, LHAG MA PHYI'I KHAMS LNGA DANG, CHOS\
KHAMS KYI PHYED DE LAS GZHAN PA RNAMS DBANG PO\
\
MA YIN PA'I PHYIR, SHES BYA CHOS CAN, CHOS MNGON PA MDZOD KYI\
KHAMS BSTAN PA ZHES BYA BA'I GNAS DANG PO LEGS PAR GTAN LA PHAB\
PA YIN TE, MDOR BSTAN RGYAS BSHAD RNAMS\
\
TSIG DON DANG SBYI DON MTHA' DPYAD PA GSUM GYIS LEGS PAR BKRAL\
BA'I PHYIR, ,SMRAS PA, CHOS MNGON RIN CHEN MANG 'DREN LEGS BSHAD\
KHUR LCI GSER GYI SHING RTA CHER, ,LUNG RIGS\
\
NOR BU SNA TSOGS SGRA DON HA RI'I SKUD BAR BSTAR BYAS PAS, ,DRA\
BA'I TSOGS MANG SGRA SNYAN SIL SIL DRIL 'KHROL GZHI LNGA'I RI MO\
BKRA, ,GANG 'DI LONGS SHIG DGA' BDE'I NOR DANG GTAN 'DUN DON\
\
KUN 'GRUB, ,BLO CHUNG MA SBYANGS ZER SGROS PA YI SBRA, ,CUNG ZAD\
SBYANGS PA'I SRIN BU'I DAR SKUD DANG, ,CHOS MNGON LHA RDZAS RIN\
CHEN SKUD PA GSUM, ,GCIG TU MA 'DZIN MCHOG\
